/bin/zsh -lc "cat > quality/QUALITY.md <<'EOF'
# Quality Constitution: ZINC-FUSION-V16
> Generated by [Quality Playbook](https://github.com/andrewstellman/quality-playbook) v1.5.6 — Andrew Stellman
> Date: 2026-05-16 · Project: ZINC-FUSION-V16

## Purpose

Quality for ZINC-FUSION-V16 means procurement decisions are safe to act on under real market volatility, not just that routes return HTTP 200. Data freshness, contract consistency, and horizon alignment must stay correct across ingest SQL, API handlers, and dashboard rendering.

Deming applies here as an engineering workflow rule: quality is built into artifacts that every future AI or human session must inherit ("'`QUALITY.md`, `REQUIREMENTS.md`, protocol docs, and functional tests). Juran applies as fitness-for-use: Chris and Kevin need reliable ZL price-level intelligence to make buy/wait decisions. Crosby applies as operational cost control: one hour spent preventing silent freshness drift is cheaper than a week of bad procurement timing.

## Coverage Targets

| Subsystem | Target | Why |
|---|---:|---|
| `ops.ingest_run` cross-writer contract | 95% | Inconsistent run telemetry can hide ingest failure and break incident response. |
| Auth and verification gate policy | 90% | `/api/cron` assumptions can reintroduce forbidden architecture or block compliant releases. |
| ZL API envelope family | 90% | Divergent envelope semantics create false parity failures and brittle client behavior. |
| Risk-factor freshness and mixed-vintage signaling | 92% | Stale freshness presentation can mislead procurement timing. |
| Forecast horizon normalization | 95% | Horizon drift across forecast surfaces breaks chart/target/probability parity. |
| AI snapshot ingest and fallback signaling | 90% | Silent snapshot rejection degrades AI-first cards without operator visibility. |
| Pipeline readiness signaling | 85% | Scaffold phases in `--all` runs can overstate production readiness. |

## Coverage Theater Prevention

- Passing tests that only assert `ok: true` without validating envelope shape.
- Testing fallback code by asserting output exists, but not asserting downgrade indicators.
- Source-inspection tests that never run (`run=False`, disabled guards left in place forever).
- Tests that verify only one forecast endpoint while claiming horizon consistency for three endpoints.
- Mock-only ingest tests that never verify shared table contract fields (`run_id`, status vocabulary).
- Gate scripts that check legacy route shapes (`/api/cron`) instead of architecture policy.
- Freshness tests that verify one date field but ignore mixed-vintage semantics.

## Fitness-to-Purpose Scenarios

### Scenario 1: Ingest Telemetry Contract Split

**Requirement tag:** [Req: inferred — REQ-001]

**What happened:** `ops.ingest_run` requires `run_id`, but legacy SQL writers insert rows without it while TS helpers write uppercase status enums. This permits partial observability and fragmented status semantics across the same table.

**The requirement:** All ingest writers must use one lifecycle contract: explicit `run_id`, canonical status vocabulary, and deterministic start/success/failure transitions.

**How to verify:** `test_req001_all_ingest_writers_include_run_id_and_canonical_status` in `quality/test_functional.py`.

### Scenario 2: Forbidden Cron Surface Drift

**Requirement tag:** [Req: inferred — REQ-002]

**What happened:** Architecture policy forbids Vercel cron routes, but middleware and verification logic still encode `/api/cron` assumptions. This can block compliant builds or push engineers toward forbidden route resurrection.

**The requirement:** Auth middleware and verification gates must validate pg_cron-only architecture without requiring `/api/cron` endpoints.

**How to verify:** `test_req002_no_runtime_or_gate_dependency_on_api_cron_path` in `quality/test_functional.py`.

### Scenario 3: Intraday Fallback Promise Divergence

**Requirement tag:** [Req: inferred — REQ-003]

**What happened:** `/api/zl/intraday` claims a 15m→1m fallback in comments while querying only `mkt.price_15m`. Consumers can trust resilience that is not implemented.

**The requirement:** Either implement fallback behavior to `mkt.price_1m` or remove fallback claims and align client assumptions.

**How to verify:** `test_req003_intraday_route_contract_matches_implemented_fallback` in `quality/test_functional.py`.

### Scenario 4: Envelope Contract Drift Across Surfaces

**Requirement tag:** [Req: inferred — REQ-004]

**What happened:** Route responses, shared API contract types, and parity gate checks disagree about optional vs required envelope fields (`warning`, shape differences). False-negative parity failures can mask real regressions.

**The requirement:** Contract types, route envelopes, and verification scripts must share one consistent envelope policy.

**How to verify:** `test_req004_contract_and_gate_align_on_warning_semantics` in `quality/test_functional.py`.

### Scenario 5: Mixed-Vintage Freshness Misread

**Requirement tag:** [Req: inferred — REQ-005]

**What happened:** Risk-factor API sets canonical `as_of_date` to oldest component date while also exposing min/max range. Dashboard messaging can be interpreted as fully stale even when only part of vector is stale.

**The requirement:** Mixed-vintage data must be explicitly signaled as degraded with field-level transparency.

**How to verify:** `test_req005_risk_factor_payload_exposes_mixed_vintage_metadata` in `quality/test_functional.py`.

### Scenario 6: Forecast Horizon Normalization Drift

**Requirement tag:** [Req: inferred — REQ-006]

**What happened:** `normalizeHorizon` logic is duplicated across three endpoints. A one-file edit can desynchronize forecast, target-zone, and probability surfaces.

**The requirement:** Horizon normalization constants and mapping behavior must remain equivalent across all forecast-facing endpoints.

**How to verify:** `test_req006_normalize_horizon_logic_is_identical_across_three_routes` in `quality/test_functional.py`.

### Scenario 7: Snapshot Source Whitelist Regression

**Requirement tag:** [Req: inferred — REQ-004]

**What happened:** Snapshot source labels are hard-whitelisted. A source-label drift can silently null out snapshots and trigger unannounced fallback narratives.

**The requirement:** Whitelist changes must be deliberate, and fallback behavior must expose reliability downgrade cues.

**How to verify:** `test_scenario_snapshot_source_whitelist_is_explicit_and_auditable` in `quality/test_functional.py`.

### Scenario 8: Scaffold Pipeline Misreported as Ready

**Requirement tag:** [Req: inferred — REQ-001]

**What happened:** `pipeline.py --all` includes scaffold phases returning `status: scaffold`. Operators can read full-run completion as inference readiness.

**The requirement:** Scaffold status must remain explicit and blocked from “ready” interpretation until implemented.

**How to verify:** `test_scenario_pipeline_order_and_scaffold_modules_are_visible` in `quality/test_functional.py`.

## AI Session Quality Discipline

1. Read `quality/QUALITY.md` and `quality/REQUIREMENTS.md` before changing behavior.
2. Preserve every REQ `Pattern` tag in both Markdown and manifest outputs.
3. Treat cross-file consistency requirements as first-class; do not verify routes in isolation.
4. Run mechanical enumeration verification before asserting completeness claims.
5. Never classify a payload as fresh without validating mixed-vintage metadata fields.
6. Do not close a quality phase until artifacts, manifests, and receipts are all on disk.

## The Human Gate

- Procurement risk appetite decisions for stale or mixed-vintage data tolerance.
- Final severity of architecture-policy drift findings that affect release timelines.
- Decisions to standardize envelope shape vs retaining backward-compatible variants.
- Approval to change ingest status vocabulary in production tables.
- Go/no-go on interpreting scaffold pipeline phases as launch-ready.
EOF

1. [INVARIANT] `ops.ingest_run.run_id` is the primary key for ingest lifecycle rows.

3. [ERROR] Exception path updates ingest run row with `status='"'error'"'` and SQLERRM.
4. [INVARIANT] Completion path updates same `run_id` row with finish timestamp and record count.

### `lib/server/ingest-run.ts` (3 contracts)

1. [METHOD] `startIngestRun` emits `RUNNING` status with generated UUID.
2. [METHOD] `finishIngestRunSuccess` and `finishIngestRunFailure` update row by `run_id`.

2. [METHOD] Route success paths should serialize data with stable top-level fields.
3. [ERROR] Route failure paths should preserve structured error payloads.
4. [COMPAT] Parity gates should assert only contract-required fields.

### `app/api/zl/intraday/route.ts` + `supabase/migrations/202603180002_mkt.sql` (2 contracts)

### `lib/server/ai-snapshot.ts` + card routes (4 contracts)

### `app/api/zl/{forecast,target-zones,forecast-targets}/route.ts` (4 contracts)

# Behavioral Requirements — ZINC-FUSION-V16
> Generated by [Quality Playbook](https://github.com/andrewstellman/quality-playbook) v1.5.6 — Andrew Stellman
> Date: 2026-05-16 · Project: ZINC-FUSION-V16

Version: v1.0
Pipeline: contract-extraction v2 with narrative pass

## Project Overview

ZINC-FUSION-V16 is a commodity procurement forecasting platform focused on ZL futures price-level intelligence for buy-side operations. The system combines Supabase-hosted ingestion, Next.js API and UI surfaces, and a Python forecasting pipeline. Operational safety depends on contract alignment across SQL ingest writers, API envelopes, horizon normalization, and freshness semantics presented to procurement users.

This requirements set is derived from Phase 1 exploration evidence in "'`quality/EXPLORATION.md` and targets the highest-risk divergence vectors discovered there: telemetry contract split, architecture/gate drift, fallback-contract mismatch, envelope inconsistency, mixed-vintage miscommunication, and duplicated horizon logic.

## Use Cases

### UC-01: Record an ingest run lifecycle event across SQL and TS writers

- Actors: pg_cron SQL functions, API helper writer.
- Preconditions: An ingest job starts, succeeds, or fails.
- Steps:
  1. Writer allocates or receives a run identifier.
  2. Writer emits start record to `ops.ingest_run`.
  3. Writer updates same run record to terminal status and timestamps.
- Postconditions: Telemetry rows are query-consistent across writers.
- Alternative paths: On ingest failure, terminal status and error message are still written.
- Requirements: REQ-001

### UC-02: Verify architecture-compliant auth and gate behavior without cron-route dependency

- Actors: Middleware, verification scripts.
- Preconditions: Protected route request or verification run.
- Steps:
  1. Middleware enforces auth/session rules.
  2. Verification gates evaluate architecture compliance.
  3. No component assumes `/api/cron` surface exists.
- Postconditions: Compliant builds are not blocked by forbidden-route checks.
- Alternative paths: Gate outputs actionable architecture mismatch evidence.
- Requirements: REQ-002

### UC-03: Serve intraday ZL bars with deterministic fallback semantics

- Actors: `/api/zl/intraday` route.
- Preconditions: User requests intraday bars.
- Steps:
  1. Route loads primary 15m dataset.
  2. If primary unavailable, route follows explicitly documented fallback behavior.
  3. Response contract communicates the data-source path used.
- Postconditions: Client expectations match real behavior.
- Alternative paths: If no fallback exists, route and docs declare no-fallback explicitly.
- Requirements: REQ-003

### UC-04: Enforce consistent envelope contract across forecast and dashboard APIs

- Actors: API routes, contract types, parity gate scripts.
- Preconditions: Success or failure responses emitted by covered endpoints.
- Steps:
  1. Contract type declares required and optional fields.
  2. Route handlers serialize envelopes accordingly.
  3. Gate checks validate only declared requirements.
- Postconditions: Parity failures indicate product defects, not harness drift.
- Alternative paths: Endpoint-specific exceptions are documented and consistently enforced.
- Requirements: REQ-004

### UC-05: Render risk-factor freshness with transparent mixed-vintage semantics

- Actors: Risk-factor API and dashboard card UI.
- Preconditions: Component timestamps differ across factors.
- Steps:
  1. API emits min/max/as-of and mixed-vintage fields.
  2. UI shows degraded-state freshness messaging.
  3. Operator can distinguish globally stale from partially stale vectors.
- Postconditions: Procurement timing decisions use correct recency confidence.
- Alternative paths: If metadata absent, UI displays explicit unknown-freshness state.
- Requirements: REQ-005

### UC-06.a: Normalize horizon values in `/api/zl/forecast`

- Actors: Forecast route.
- Preconditions: Rows include `horizon_days` and `model_version`.
- Steps: Apply canonical allowlist and legacy remap.
- Postconditions: Returned series uses canonical horizon set.
- Requirements: REQ-006

### UC-06.b: Normalize horizon values in `/api/zl/target-zones`

- Actors: Target-zones route.
- Preconditions: Rows include `horizon_days` and `model_version`.
- Steps: Apply same normalization logic as UC-06.a.
- Postconditions: Target-zone horizons align with forecast horizons.
- Requirements: REQ-006

### UC-06.c: Normalize horizon values in `/api/zl/forecast-targets`

- Actors: Forecast-targets route.
- Preconditions: Rows include `horizon_days` and `model_version`.
- Steps: Apply same normalization logic as UC-06.a and UC-06.b.
- Postconditions: Probability-surface horizons align with other forecast surfaces.
- Requirements: REQ-006

## Cross-Cutting Concerns

- **Architecture authority:** Repository policy (`AGENTS.md`) is authoritative over historical middleware or gate assumptions.
- **Telemetry integrity:** Ingest observability must stay coherent across language boundaries (SQL and TypeScript writers).
- **Contract traceability:** API contract types, route payloads, and gate scripts must remain synchronized.
- **Degradation transparency:** Fallback and mixed-vintage behaviors must be explicit in machine and user-facing surfaces.

## Functional Sections

### Ingestion Observability and Lifecycle Contracts

#### REQ-001: `ops.ingest_run` writers MUST use one normalized run contract

- Functional section: Ingestion Observability and Lifecycle Contracts
- Tier: 3
- Pattern: parity
- References: `supabase/migrations/202603180009_ops_vegas.sql:3-14`; `supabase/migrations/20260414001_ingest_zl_intraday.sql:50-52`; `supabase/migrations/202605080003_supabase_trusted_site_fill_hourly.sql:55-57`; `lib/server/ingest-run.ts:3-4`
- Linked use cases: UC-01
- Requirement: Every SQL and TypeScript writer that inserts or updates `ops.ingest_run` MUST include stable `run_id` lifecycle semantics and one canonical status vocabulary.
- Conditions of satisfaction:
  1. `ops.ingest_run` DDL defines `run_id UUID PRIMARY KEY` and writer inserts honor that key.
  2. Each writer emits start and terminal state for the same `run_id`.
  3. Status values are normalized (no mixed uppercase/lowercase contract split).
  4. Error paths log terminal status with timestamp and error detail.

### Architecture Policy and Verification Alignment

#### REQ-002: Verification and auth scaffolding MUST not require `/api/cron`

- Functional section: Architecture Policy and Verification Alignment
- Tier: 3
- Pattern: whitelist
- References: `AGENTS.md:44-45`; `AGENTS.md:149-160`; `lib/supabase/proxy.ts:15-42`; `scripts/verify/gate3.sh:5`
- Linked use cases: UC-02
- Requirement: Middleware and verification logic MUST treat pg_cron-only architecture as authoritative and MUST NOT enforce `/api/cron` route presence.
- Conditions of satisfaction:
  1. Middleware rules do not carve out `/api/cron` behavior that contradicts architecture policy.
  2. Gate scripts verify policy-conformant surfaces instead of forbidden route patterns.
  3. Documentation and scripts share the same architecture truth source.

### Intraday Data Contract Fidelity

#### REQ-003: `/api/zl/intraday` MUST align documented fallback with implementation

- Functional section: Intraday Data Contract Fidelity
- Tier: 3
- References: `app/api/zl/intraday/route.ts:10-16`; `supabase/migrations/202603180002_mkt.sql:17-20`
- Linked use cases: UC-03
- Requirement: Intraday route behavior, comments, and consumer assumptions MUST agree on whether 1m fallback exists.
- Conditions of satisfaction:
  1. If fallback is claimed, route executes an explicit 15m→1m fallback query path.
  2. If fallback is not implemented, comments and downstream expectations state that explicitly.
  3. Response metadata identifies the effective data source path for debugging and parity checks.

### API Envelope and Parity Contract Consistency

#### REQ-004: Forecast/dashboard API surfaces, contract types, and parity harness MUST agree on envelope semantics

- Functional section: API Envelope and Parity Contract Consistency
- Tier: 3
- Pattern: parity
- References: `lib/contracts/api.ts:3-9`; `scripts/verify/gate6.sh:74-80`; `app/api/zl/live/route.ts:28-33`; `app/api/zl/target-zones/route.ts:74-79`; `app/api/zl/forecast-targets/route.ts:97-100`
- Linked use cases: UC-04
- Requirement: The shared envelope contract MUST define one source of truth for required vs optional fields and all covered routes/gates MUST enforce the same semantics.
- Conditions of satisfaction:
  1. Optional fields (for example `warning`) are optional everywhere they appear.
  2. Success/failure envelope families are documented and validated consistently.
  3. Endpoint-specific envelope exceptions are intentional, documented, and parity-tested.

### Freshness Transparency for Procurement Decisions

#### REQ-005: Risk-factor freshness MUST expose mixed-vintage state without mislabeling oldest timestamp as global freshness

- Functional section: Freshness Transparency for Procurement Decisions
- Tier: 3
- Pattern: compensation
- References: `app/api/dashboard/risk-factors/route.ts:715-719`; `app/api/dashboard/risk-factors/route.ts:815-819`; `components/dashboard/MarketRiskFactors.tsx:64-77`; `components/dashboard/MarketRiskFactors.tsx:357-358`
- Linked use cases: UC-05
- Requirement: API and UI freshness semantics MUST make degraded recency explicit when component dates diverge.
- Conditions of satisfaction:
  1. API emits `as_of_date_min`, `as_of_date_max`, and `mixed_vintage` for every payload.
  2. UI copy distinguishes mixed-vintage from globally stale data.
  3. Freshness labels do not imply full-vector recency when only subset is stale.

### Forecast Horizon Normalization Consistency

#### REQ-006: Horizon normalization MUST remain identical across all forecast-facing ZL endpoints

- Functional section: Forecast Horizon Normalization Consistency
- Tier: 3
- Pattern: parity
- References: `app/api/zl/forecast/route.ts:13-24`; `app/api/zl/target-zones/route.ts:13-24`; `app/api/zl/forecast-targets/route.ts:22-33`
- Linked use cases: UC-06.a, UC-06.b, UC-06.c
- Requirement: `normalizeHorizon` allowlist and legacy remap behavior MUST remain equivalent for forecast, target-zones, and forecast-targets endpoints.
- Conditions of satisfaction:
  1. Each endpoint uses identical `AG_HORIZON_DAYS` and `LEGACY_HORIZON_MAP` definitions.
  2. Legacy model versions apply the same remap (`7→30`, `14→90`, `30→180`).
  3. Unknown horizons are filtered consistently and logged consistently.
EOF

# Code Review Protocol: ZINC-FUSION-V16
> Generated by [Quality Playbook](https://github.com/andrewstellman/quality-playbook) v1.5.6 — Andrew Stellman
> Date: 2026-05-16 · Project: ZINC-FUSION-V16

## Bootstrap (Read First)

Before review, read:
1. "'`quality/QUALITY.md`
2. `quality/REQUIREMENTS.md`
3. `quality/EXPLORATION.md`
4. `AGENTS.md`
5. `docs/plans/2026-03-17-v16-migration-plan.md`

## Pass 1: Structural Review

Review code for correctness defects only. No style feedback.

### Mandatory guardrails

- Line numbers required for every finding.
- Read function bodies, not signatures only.
- Use `QUESTION` if confidence is insufficient.
- Grep before claiming absence.
- No refactor/style findings.

### Required scrutiny areas

1. Input validation and trust boundaries (API envelopes, whitelist gates, fallback routing).
2. Resource lifecycle (ingest run creation/update and terminal states).
3. Concurrency/state integrity (run lifecycle transitions, status updates, stale-metadata propagation).
4. Unit/encoding correctness (date semantics, horizon values, envelope field types).
5. Enumeration/whitelist completeness with mechanical two-list diff.

### Project-specific structural targets

- `supabase/migrations/20260414001_ingest_zl_intraday.sql`
- `supabase/migrations/202605080003_supabase_trusted_site_fill_hourly.sql`
- `lib/server/ingest-run.ts`
- `lib/supabase/proxy.ts`
- `scripts/verify/gate3.sh`, `scripts/verify/gate6.sh`
- `app/api/zl/{intraday,forecast,target-zones,forecast-targets}/route.ts`
- `app/api/dashboard/risk-factors/route.ts`
- `lib/server/ai-snapshot.ts`

## Pass 2: Requirement Verification

Evaluate each REQ individually using `quality/REQUIREMENTS.md`.

For each REQ, output:

- `Status:` SATISFIED / VIOLATED / PARTIALLY SATISFIED / NOT ASSESSABLE
- `Evidence:` file:line references
- `Analysis:` expected vs observed behavior
- `Severity:` required for VIOLATED/PARTIALLY SATISFIED

### REQ verification checklist

- REQ-001: Confirm all ingest writers satisfy unified `run_id` + status contract.
- REQ-002: Confirm no middleware/gate dependency on `/api/cron`.
- REQ-003: Confirm intraday fallback behavior and contract text alignment.
- REQ-004: Confirm envelope contract parity across types/routes/gates.
- REQ-005: Confirm mixed-vintage freshness semantics are explicit and non-misleading.
- REQ-006: Confirm identical normalization logic across all forecast surfaces.

## Pass 3: Cross-Requirement Consistency

Check shared concepts across REQ pairs.

Required pairings:

- REQ-001 vs REQ-004: shared ingest/API contract normalization principles.
- REQ-002 vs REQ-004: gate policy consistency with architecture authority.
- REQ-004 vs REQ-006: forecast surface consistency (envelope + horizon semantics).
- REQ-003 vs REQ-005: degradation/fallback communication consistency.

For each pair, report CONSISTENT or INCONSISTENT with file:line evidence.

## Mechanical Enumeration Rules

If a finding claims whitelist/dispatch completeness, reviewer MUST:

1. Use `quality/mechanical/*` extraction artifacts when available.
2. Compare extracted code list vs authoritative list.
3. Cite exact case/entry lines.
4. Mark any missing entry as BUG candidate.

## Regression Test Closure Mandate

Every confirmed BUG requires one of:

- A regression test in `quality/test_regression.*` with expected-failure guard.
- An explicit exemption rationale in review output.

Patch artifacts required per confirmed bug:

- `quality/patches/BUG-NNN-regression-test.patch` (mandatory)
- `quality/patches/BUG-NNN-fix.patch` (strongly encouraged)

## Combined Summary Output Format

| Source | Finding | Severity | Status | Regression test / Exemption |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| Pass 1 | ... | ... | BUG/QUESTION | ... |
| Pass 2 (REQ-NNN) | ... | ... | VIOLATED/... | ... |
| Pass 3 (REQ-X vs REQ-Y) | ... | ... | INCONSISTENT/... | ... |

Final recommendation options:

- `SHIP`
- `FIX BEFORE MERGE`
- `BLOCK`
EOF

# Integration Test Protocol: ZINC-FUSION-V16
> Generated by [Quality Playbook](https://github.com/andrewstellman/quality-playbook) v1.5.6 — Andrew Stellman
> Date: 2026-05-16 · Project: ZINC-FUSION-V16

## Working Directory

Run all commands from repository root using relative paths.

## Safety Constraints

- Do not modify source code during integration runs.
- Write outputs only under "'`quality/results/`.
- Record failures; do not auto-fix while executing this protocol.

## Pre-Flight Check

- [ ] `quality/REQUIREMENTS.md` exists and includes UC-01..UC-06 identifiers.
- [ ] `quality/test_functional.py` exists.
- [ ] Python test dependencies available for `unittest` run.
- [ ] Shell verifier scripts executable (`quality/mechanical/verify.sh`).
- [ ] Supabase/network dependent checks are scoped as non-destructive read-only validations.

## Field Reference Table (built from code contracts)

### API envelope contract (`lib/contracts/api.ts`)

| Field | Type | Constraints |
|---|---|---|
| `ok` | boolean | Required in canonical envelope |
| `data` | generic payload | Optional when `error` present |
| `error` | string | Optional when success |
| `warning` | string | Optional; MUST remain optional across gate checks |

### Risk-factor freshness payload (`app/api/dashboard/risk-factors/route.ts`)

| Field | Type | Constraints |
|---|---|---|
| `as_of_date` | string/date | Must not misrepresent mixed-vintage payload as globally fresh |
| `as_of_date_min` | string/date | Required for mixed-vintage transparency |
| `as_of_date_max` | string/date | Required for mixed-vintage transparency |
| `mixed_vintage` | boolean | Required degraded-mode indicator |

### Forecast horizon normalization surfaces (`app/api/zl/*`)

| Field | Type | Constraints |
|---|---|---|
| `horizon_days` | integer | Canonical set `[30,90,180]` after normalization |
| `model_version` | string | `legacy` triggers remap `7→30`, `14→90`, `30→180` |

## Test Matrix

| Group | Use-case traceability | Check | Method | Pass Criteria |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| 1 | UC-01 | Ingest run contract parity | `python -m unittest quality.test_functional.SpecRequirementsFunctionalTest.test_req001_all_ingest_writers_include_run_id_and_canonical_status` | All writers satisfy unified lifecycle contract |
| 2 | UC-02 | Cron-policy gate alignment | `python -m unittest quality.test_functional.SpecRequirementsFunctionalTest.test_req002_no_runtime_or_gate_dependency_on_api_cron_path` | No hard dependency on `/api/cron` |
| 3 | UC-03 | Intraday fallback contract fidelity | `python -m unittest quality.test_functional.SpecRequirementsFunctionalTest.test_req003_intraday_route_contract_matches_implemented_fallback` | Contract text matches implemented fallback behavior |
| 4 | UC-04 | Envelope parity contract | `python -m unittest quality.test_functional.SpecRequirementsFunctionalTest.test_req004_contract_and_gate_align_on_warning_semantics` | Route, type contract, and gate semantics align |
| 5 | UC-05 | Freshness transparency | `python -m unittest quality.test_functional.SpecRequirementsFunctionalTest.test_req005_risk_factor_payload_exposes_mixed_vintage_metadata` | Mixed-vintage fields always present |
| 6 | UC-06.a, UC-06.b | Horizon normalization parity (forecast + target-zones) | `python -m unittest quality.test_functional.SpecRequirementsFunctionalTest.test_req006_normalize_horizon_logic_is_identical_across_three_routes` | Shared normalization logic is equivalent |
| 7 | UC-06.c | Horizon map continuity (forecast-targets) | `bash quality/mechanical/verify.sh` | Mechanical extracts match saved artifacts |
| 8 | [Infrastructure] | Functional suite smoke run | `python -m unittest quality/test_functional.py` | Test harness executes and reports deterministic output |

Each group maps to at most 2 use cases.

## Automated Integration Execution

```bash
mkdir -p quality/results
python -m unittest quality/test_functional.py 2>&1 | tee quality/results/integration-functional.log
bash quality/mechanical/verify.sh 2>&1 | tee quality/results/integration-mechanical.log
```

Validate selectors before use:

```bash
python -m unittest -k req001 quality.test_functional >/dev/null
python -m unittest -k req006 quality.test_functional >/dev/null
```

If selector discovery fails due environment issues, mark group result `error` with `pre_flight_error: environment`.

|---|---|---|---|---|

# Spec Audit Protocol: ZINC-FUSION-V16
> Generated by [Quality Playbook](https://github.com/andrewstellman/quality-playbook) v1.5.6 — Andrew Stellman
> Date: 2026-05-16 · Project: ZINC-FUSION-V16

## The Definitive Audit Prompt

Run this exact prompt with three independent auditors.

---

**Context files to read:**
1. "'`quality/QUALITY.md`
2. `quality/REQUIREMENTS.md`
3. `quality/EXPLORATION.md`
4. `AGENTS.md`
5. `docs/plans/2026-03-17-v16-migration-plan.md`

**Task:** Act as the Tester. Compare implementation against requirements. Report only defects.

**Rules:**
- Every finding must include file:line evidence.
- Grep before claiming missing behavior.
- Read full function body before claiming behavior exists.
- Classify each finding as `MISSING`, `DIVERGENT`, `UNDOCUMENTED`, or `PHANTOM`.
- Use requirement tags in output (`REQ-001`..`REQ-006`).

**Project-specific scrutiny areas:**
1. Cross-writer `ops.ingest_run` lifecycle consistency (`run_id`, status vocabulary, terminal updates).
2. `/api/cron` assumptions in middleware and gate scripts vs architecture policy.
3. `/api/zl/intraday` fallback promise vs executed query paths.
4. Envelope semantics between `lib/contracts/api.ts`, route handlers, and `gate6.sh`.
5. Risk-factor freshness semantics and mixed-vintage messaging continuity API→UI.
6. Horizon normalization parity across forecast, target-zones, and forecast-targets routes.
7. Snapshot whitelist rejection behavior and fallback observability.

**Output format:**

### file/path.ext
- **Line NNN:** [MISSING/DIVERGENT/UNDOCUMENTED/PHANTOM] [REQ-NNN] defect summary.
  Spec says: ...
  Code does: ...

---

## Pre-audit docs validation (required triage section)

`reference_docs/` is absent for this run.

Use this exact section header in triage:

`## Pre-audit docs validation`

Required content:
- State “No supplemental docs provided. Auditors relied on in-repo specs and code only.”
- Note any claim from generated artifacts that cannot be confirmed in source.

## Running the Audit

1. Execute prompt against three models independently.
2. Save raw outputs:
   - `quality/spec_audits/YYYY-MM-DD-auditor1.md`
   - `quality/spec_audits/YYYY-MM-DD-auditor2.md`
   - `quality/spec_audits/YYYY-MM-DD-auditor3.md`
3. Produce triage:
   - `quality/spec_audits/YYYY-MM-DD-triage.md`

## Council Status Block (mandatory)

Triage must start with:

```markdown
## Council Status
- Auditor 1: Fresh report received (YYYY-MM-DD)
- Auditor 2: Fresh report received (YYYY-MM-DD)
- Auditor 3: Fresh report received (YYYY-MM-DD)
```

If fewer than 3 reports are usable, explicitly log effective council size.

## Confidence and Triage Rules

| Confidence | Found By | Action |
|---|---|---|
| Highest | 3/3 | Confirm unless verification probe disproves |
| High | 2/3 | Confirm with targeted verification |
| Needs verification | 1/3 | Run verification probe before classification |

## Verification Probes Must Be Executable

For disputed findings, create executable assertions in one of:

- `quality/mechanical/verify.sh`, or
- `quality/spec_audits/triage_probes.sh`

Requirements:
- Rejections require passing assertions proving claim false.
- Confirmations require failing assertions proving claim true.
- Every assertion cites exact evidence line.

## Categorize Confirmed Findings

Use one of:
- Spec bug
- Design decision
- Real code bug
- Documentation gap
- Missing test
- Inferred requirement wrong

## Cross-Artifact Consistency

Compare triage against Phase 3 code review findings.
If conflict exists on same factual claim, run verification probe and record resolution.

## Fix Execution Rules

- Group fixes by subsystem.
- Avoid mega-prompts.
- Require regression tests for real code bugs.

## Output Artifacts

- `quality/spec_audits/YYYY-MM-DD-auditor*.md`
- `quality/spec_audits/YYYY-MM-DD-triage.md`
- `quality/spec_audits/triage_probes.sh` (if probes used)
EOF

# TDD Verification Protocol: ZINC-FUSION-V16
> Generated by [Quality Playbook](https://github.com/andrewstellman/quality-playbook) v1.5.6 — Andrew Stellman
> Date: 2026-05-16 · Project: ZINC-FUSION-V16

## Scope

Run red/green verification for every confirmed bug in "'`quality/BUGS.md`.

## Spec-grounded test requirements

For each BUG-NNN:

1. Read associated requirement (`REQ-NNN`) from `quality/REQUIREMENTS.md`.
2. Read bug `spec basis` field.
3. Build assertions using spec language (not internal-only shorthand).
4. Add traceability comment with requirement ID, bug ID, and spec passage.

## Red-Green Execution

For each bug with regression and fix patches:

1. **Red phase:** run regression test on unpatched code. Expected: fail.
2. **Green phase:** apply fix patch and rerun same test. Expected: pass.
3. **Record:** write logs and update closure status.

If no fix patch exists:
- Red phase still required.
- Green phase marked `skipped`.
- Verdict is `confirmed open`.

## Framework adaptation

Project baseline test framework: Python `unittest`.

Primary command pattern:

```bash
python -m unittest quality.test_regression
```

For per-bug runs:

```bash
python -m unittest quality.test_regression.TestRegression.test_bug_nnn
```

## Required Log Artifacts

For each confirmed BUG-NNN:

- `quality/results/BUG-NNN.red.log`
- `quality/results/BUG-NNN.green.log` (if fix patch exists)

First line must be one of: `RED`, `GREEN`, `NOT_RUN`, `ERROR`.

## Log Template

```text
RED
--- Test output for BUG-NNN red phase ---
Command: python -m unittest quality.test_regression.TestRegression.test_bug_nnn
Exit code: 1
[stdout/stderr]
```

```json
      "patch_gate_passed": true,
      "writeup_path": "quality/writeups/BUG-001.md",
      "junit_red": "tdd-red-BUG-001.xml",
      "junit_green": "tdd-green-BUG-001.xml",
      "junit_available": false,
      "notes": ""
    }
  ],
  "summary": {
    "total": 1,
    "verified": 1,
    "confirmed_open": 0,
    "red_failed": 0,
    "green_failed": 0
  }
}
```

Allowed verdicts:
- `TDD verified`
- `red failed`
- `green failed`
- `confirmed open`
- `deferred`

cat > quality/mechanical/verify.sh <<'EOF'
#"'!/usr/bin/env bash
# Generated by Quality Playbook v1.5.6 — https://github.com/andrewstellman/quality-playbook
# Author: Andrew Stellman · Date: 2026-05-16 · Project: ZINC-FUSION-V16

set -euo pipefail

ROOT="$(cd "$(dirname "${BASH_SOURCE[0]}")/../.." && pwd)"
MECH="$ROOT/quality/mechanical"
TMP="$(mktemp -d)"
trap '"'rm -rf \""'$TMP"'"' EXIT

check_snapshot() {
  local generated=\""'$1"
  local baseline="$2"
  if diff -u "$baseline" "$generated" >/dev/null; then
    echo "PASS  $(basename "$baseline")"
  else
    echo "FAIL  $(basename "$baseline")"
    diff -u "$baseline" "$generated"
    return 1
  fi
}

# 1) Trusted snapshot source whitelist
awk '"'/TRUSTED_SNAPSHOT_SOURCES/{capture=1} capture{print} /\\]\\);/{if(capture){capture=0; exit}}' \""'$ROOT/lib/server/ai-snapshot.ts" '"\\
  | rg -o '\"["'^"]+"'"' \\
  | tr -d '\"' \\
  > \""'$TMP/trusted_snapshot_sources.txt"
check_snapshot "$TMP/trusted_snapshot_sources.txt" "$MECH/trusted_snapshot_sources.txt"

# 2) Horizon normalization blocks across route family
rg -n '"'const AG_HORIZON_DAYS|const LEGACY_HORIZON_MAP|function normalizeHorizon|if \\(modelVersion === \"legacy\"\\)|return AG_HORIZON_DAYS.has' \""'$ROOT/app/api/zl/forecast/route.ts" '"\\
  > \""'$TMP/forecast_normalize_horizon.txt"
check_snapshot "$TMP/forecast_normalize_horizon.txt" "$MECH/forecast_normalize_horizon.txt"

rg -n '"'const AG_HORIZON_DAYS|const LEGACY_HORIZON_MAP|function normalizeHorizon|if \\(modelVersion === \"legacy\"\\)|return AG_HORIZON_DAYS.has' \""'$ROOT/app/api/zl/target-zones/route.ts" '"\\
  > \""'$TMP/target_zones_normalize_horizon.txt"
check_snapshot "$TMP/target_zones_normalize_horizon.txt" "$MECH/target_zones_normalize_horizon.txt"

rg -n '"'const AG_HORIZON_DAYS|const LEGACY_HORIZON_MAP|function normalizeHorizon|if \\(modelVersion === \"legacy\"\\)|return AG_HORIZON_DAYS.has' \""'$ROOT/app/api/zl/forecast-targets/route.ts" '"\\
  > \""'$TMP/forecast_targets_normalize_horizon.txt"
check_snapshot "$TMP/forecast_targets_normalize_horizon.txt" "$MECH/forecast_targets_normalize_horizon.txt"

# 3) Envelope warning semantics across contract and gate
rg -n '"'ApiEnvelope|ApiErrorEnvelope|warning' \""'$ROOT/lib/contracts/api.ts" '"\\
  > \""'$TMP/api_contract_warning_fields.txt"
check_snapshot "$TMP/api_contract_warning_fields.txt" "$MECH/api_contract_warning_fields.txt"

rg -n '"'warning|jq|gate6' \""'$ROOT/scripts/verify/gate6.sh" '"\\
  > \""'$TMP/gate6_warning_checks.txt"
check_snapshot "$TMP/gate6_warning_checks.txt" "$MECH/gate6_warning_checks.txt"

echo "Mechanical verification complete"
EOF
chmod +x quality/mechanical/verify.sh

cat > quality/test_functional.py <<'"'EOF'
# Generated by Quality Playbook v1.5.6 — https://github.com/andrewstellman/quality-playbook
# Author: Andrew Stellman · Date: 2026-05-16 · Project: ZINC-FUSION-V16

from __future__ import annotations

import re
import unittest
from pathlib import Path


REPO_ROOT = Path(__file__).resolve().parents[1]


def read_text(rel_path: str) -> str:
    return (REPO_ROOT / rel_path).read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\", errors=\"replace\")


class SpecRequirementsFunctionalTest(unittest.TestCase):
    def test_req001_all_ingest_writers_include_run_id_and_canonical_status(self) -> None:
        \"\"\"[Req: inferred — REQ-001] All ingest writers use unified run-id lifecycle contract.\"\"\"
        ddl = read_text(\"supabase/migrations/202603180009_ops_vegas.sql\")
        legacy_ingest = read_text(\"supabase/migrations/20260414001_ingest_zl_intraday.sql\")
        trusted_ingest = read_text(\"supabase/migrations/202605080003_supabase_trusted_site_fill_hourly.sql\")
        ts_writer = read_text(\"lib/server/ingest-run.ts\")

        self.assertRegex(ddl, r\"run_id\\s+UUID\\s+PRIMARY\\s+KEY\")
        self.assertIn(\"run_id\", trusted_ingest)
        self.assertIn(\"run_id\", ts_writer)
        # Desired-state assertion: legacy SQL writer should also include run_id inserts.
        self.assertRegex(legacy_ingest, r\"INSERT INTO ops\\.ingest_run \\(run_id,\")

    def test_req002_no_runtime_or_gate_dependency_on_api_cron_path(self) -> None:
        \"\"\"[Req: inferred — REQ-002] Cron route shape is not required by middleware or verification gates.\"\"\"
        proxy = read_text(\"lib/supabase/proxy.ts\")
        gate3 = read_text(\"scripts/verify/gate3.sh\")
        agents = read_text(\"AGENTS.md\")

        self.assertIn(\"No Inngest. No Vercel Cron.\", agents)
        self.assertNotIn(\"/api/cron/\", proxy)
        self.assertNotRegex(gate3, r\"rg\\s+app/api/cron\")

    def test_req003_intraday_route_contract_matches_implemented_fallback(self) -> None:
        \"\"\"[Req: inferred — REQ-003] Intraday fallback comments match executable query behavior.\"\"\"
        route = read_text(\"app/api/zl/intraday/route.ts\")
        self.assertIn(\"fallback\", route.lower())
        self.assertIn(\"mkt.price_15m\", route)
        # Desired-state assertion: explicit query path to 1m source exists when fallback is documented.
        self.assertIn(\"mkt.price_1m\", route)

    def test_req004_contract_and_gate_align_on_warning_semantics(self) -> None:
        \"\"\"[Req: inferred — REQ-004] Optional warning semantics are consistent across contract and parity gates.\"\"\"
        api_contract = read_text(\"lib/contracts/api.ts\")
        gate6 = read_text(\"scripts/verify/gate6.sh\")

        self.assertRegex(api_contract, r\"warning\\?:\\s*string\")
        # Desired-state assertion: gate should not require warning on every success payload.
        self.assertNotRegex(gate6, r'\\.warning\\s*\\|\\|\\s*empty')

    def test_req005_risk_factor_payload_exposes_mixed_vintage_metadata(self) -> None:
        \"\"\"[Req: inferred — REQ-005] Mixed-vintage freshness metadata is emitted and rendered.\"\"\"
        api = read_text(\"app/api/dashboard/risk-factors/route.ts\")
        ui = read_text(\"components/dashboard/MarketRiskFactors.tsx\")

        for field in [\"as_of_date\", \"as_of_date_min\", \"as_of_date_max\", \"mixed_vintage\"]:
            self.assertIn(field, api)
        self.assertRegex(ui, r\"mixed[-_ ]vintage|as_of_date_min|as_of_date_max\")

    def test_req006_normalize_horizon_logic_is_identical_across_three_routes(self) -> None:
        \"\"\"[Req: inferred — REQ-006] Horizon normalization logic remains equivalent across forecast surfaces.\"\"\"
        files = {
            \"forecast\": \"app/api/zl/forecast/route.ts\",
            \"target_zones\": \"app/api/zl/target-zones/route.ts\",
            \"forecast_targets\": \"app/api/zl/forecast-targets/route.ts\",
        }

        extracted: dict[str, list[str]] = {}
        pattern = re.compile(
            r\"const AG_HORIZON_DAYS|const LEGACY_HORIZON_MAP|function normalizeHorizon|if \\(modelVersion === \\\"legacy\\\"\\)|return AG_HORIZON_DAYS\\.has\",
        )
        for key, rel in files.items():
            lines = []
            for line in read_text(rel).splitlines():
                if pattern.search(line):
                    lines.append(line.strip())
            extracted[key] = lines

        self.assertEqual(extracted[\"forecast\"], extracted[\"target_zones\"])
        self.assertEqual(extracted[\"forecast\"], extracted[\"forecast_targets\"])


class FitnessScenarioFunctionalTest(unittest.TestCase):
    def test_scenario_snapshot_source_whitelist_is_explicit_and_auditable(self) -> None:
        \"\"\"[Req: inferred — REQ-004] Snapshot source whitelist is explicit and finite.\"\"\"
        text = read_text(\"lib/server/ai-snapshot.ts\")
        values = re.findall(r'\"(strategy|sentiment|legislation|vegas-intel)\"', text)
        self.assertEqual(sorted(set(values)), [\"legislation\", \"sentiment\", \"strategy\", \"vegas-intel\"])

    def test_scenario_pipeline_order_and_scaffold_modules_are_visible(self) -> None:
        \"\"\"[Req: inferred — REQ-001] Scaffold phases remain explicit in pipeline orchestration.\"\"\"
        pipeline = read_text(\"python/fusion/pipeline.py\")
        forecast = read_text(\"python/fusion/generate_forward_forecasts.py\")
        garch = read_text(\"python/fusion/run_garch.py\")
        monte = read_text(\"python/fusion/run_monte_carlo.py\")
        zones = read_text(\"python/fusion/generate_target_zones.py\")

        for phase in [\"forecast\", \"garch\", \"monte-carlo\", \"target-zones\"]:
            self.assertIn(phase, pipeline)

        self.assertIn(\"status\":=\" if False else \"status\", forecast)
        self.assertIn(\"scaffold\", forecast)
        self.assertIn(\"scaffold\", garch)
        self.assertIn(\"scaffold\", monte)
        self.assertIn(\"scaffold\", zones)

    def test_scenario_freshness_ui_does_not_drop_mixed_vintage_context(self) -> None:
        \"\"\"[Req: inferred — REQ-005] UI keeps mixed-vintage context near freshness labels.\"\"\"
        ui = read_text(\"components/dashboard/MarketRiskFactors.tsx\")
        self.assertRegex(ui, r\"as_of_date|max|min|mixed\")


class BoundaryAndEdgeCasesFunctionalTest(unittest.TestCase):
    def test_boundary_horizon_allowlist_contains_only_canonical_values(self) -> None:
        \"\"\"[Req: inferred — REQ-006] Canonical horizon allowlist remains [30, 90, 180].\"\"\"
        for rel in [
            \"app/api/zl/forecast/route.ts\",
            \"app/api/zl/target-zones/route.ts\",
            \"app/api/zl/forecast-targets/route.ts\",
        ]:
            text = read_text(rel)
            self.assertRegex(text, r\"new Set\\(\\[30,\\s*90,\\s*180\\]\\)\")

    def test_boundary_legacy_horizon_map_is_preserved(self) -> None:
        \"\"\"[Req: inferred — REQ-006] Legacy map preserves 7→30, 14→90, 30→180.\"\"\"
        text = read_text(\"app/api/zl/forecast/route.ts\")
        self.assertIn(\"7: 30\", text)
        self.assertIn(\"14: 90\", text)
        self.assertIn(\"30: 180\", text)

    def test_boundary_proxy_helper_still_handles_nextjs_internal_paths(self) -> None:
        \"\"\"[Req: inferred — REQ-002] Middleware keeps internal Next.js exceptions while avoiding cron-route dependency.\"\"\"
        proxy = read_text(\"lib/supabase/proxy.ts\")
        self.assertRegex(proxy, r\"/_next|favicon|static\")

    unittest.main()
